<td class="mbox-image"><a href="/wiki/File:Commons-logo.svg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/4/4a/Commons-logo.svg/30px-Commons-logo.svg.png" width="30" height="40" class="noviewer" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/4/4a/Commons-logo.svg/45px-Commons-logo.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/4/4a/Commons-logo.svg/59px-Commons-logo.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1024" data-file-height="1376" /></a></td>
<td class="mbox-text plainlist">Wikimedia Commons has media related to <i><b><a href="https://commons.wikimedia.org/wiki/Category:1993" class="extiw" title="commons:Category:1993">1993</a></b></i>.</td>
</tr>
</table>
<p><b>1993 (<a href="/wiki/Roman_numerals" title="Roman numerals">MCMXCIII</a>)</b> was a <a href="/wiki/Common_year" title="Common year">common year</a> <a href="/wiki/Common_year_starting_on_Friday" title="Common year starting on Friday">starting on Friday</a> (<a href="/wiki/Dominical_letter" title="Dominical letter">dominical letter</a> C) of the <a href="/wiki/Gregorian_calendar" title="Gregorian calendar">Gregorian calendar</a>, the 1993rd year of the <a href="/wiki/Common_Era" title="Common Era">Common Era</a> (CE) and <i><a href="/wiki/Anno_Domini" title="Anno Domini">Anno Domini</a></i> (AD) designations, the 993rd year of the <a href="/wiki/2nd_millennium" title="2nd millennium">2nd&#160;millennium</a>, the 93rd year of the <a href="/wiki/20th_century" title="20th century">20th&#160;century</a>, and the 4th year of the <a href="/wiki/1990s" title="1990s">1990s</a> decade.</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Events">Events</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1993&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Events">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="January">January</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1993&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: January">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:202px;"><a href="/wiki/File:44_Bill_Clinton_3x4.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/49/44_Bill_Clinton_3x4.jpg/200px-44_Bill_Clinton_3x4.jpg" width="200" height="267" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/49/44_Bill_Clinton_3x4.jpg/300px-44_Bill_Clinton_3x4.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/49/44_Bill_Clinton_3x4.jpg/400px-44_Bill_Clinton_3x4.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2103" data-file-height="2804" /></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:44_Bill_Clinton_3x4.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
<a href="/wiki/January_20" title="January 20">January 20</a>: <a href="/wiki/Bill_Clinton" title="Bill Clinton">Bill Clinton</a> is 42nd <a href="/wiki/President_of_the_United_States" title="President of the United States">President of the United States</a></div>
</div>
</div>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_1" title="January 1">January 1</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Czechoslovakia" title="Czechoslovakia">Czechoslovakia</a> ceases to exist as the <a href="/wiki/Czech_Republic" title="Czech Republic">Czech Republic</a> and <a href="/wiki/Slovakia" title="Slovakia">Slovakia</a> separate in the so-called <a href="/wiki/Dissolution_of_Czechoslovakia" title="Dissolution of Czechoslovakia">Velvet Divorce</a>.</li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/European_Economic_Community" title="European Economic Community">European Economic Community</a> eliminates trade barriers and creates a European <a href="/wiki/Single_market" title="Single market">single market</a>.</li>
<li>British <a href="/wiki/ITV_(TV_network)" title="ITV (TV network)">ITV</a> companies <a href="/wiki/GMTV" title="GMTV">GMTV</a>, <a href="/wiki/Carlton_Television" title="Carlton Television">Carlton Television</a>, <a href="/wiki/Meridian_Broadcasting" class="mw-redirect" title="Meridian Broadcasting">Meridian Broadcasting</a> and <a href="/wiki/Westcountry_Television" class="mw-redirect" title="Westcountry Television">Westcountry Television</a> start broadcasting, replacing <a href="/wiki/TV-am" title="TV-am">TV-am</a>, <a href="/wiki/Thames_Television" title="Thames Television">Thames Television</a>, <a href="/wiki/Television_South" title="Television South">TVS</a> and <a href="/wiki/Television_South_West" title="Television South West">TSW</a> respectively.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Euronews" title="Euronews">Euronews</a>, a <a href="/wiki/Multilingualism" title="Multilingualism">multilingual</a> television news channels in <a href="/wiki/Europe" title="Europe">Europe</a>, officially launched.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (December 2016)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_2" title="January 2">January 2</a> – <a href="/wiki/Sri_Lankan_Civil_War" title="Sri Lankan Civil War">Sri Lankan Civil War</a>: The <a href="/wiki/Sri_Lanka_Navy" title="Sri Lanka Navy">Sri Lanka Navy</a> <a href="/wiki/Jaffna_lagoon_massacre" title="Jaffna lagoon massacre">kills</a> 35-100 civilians on the <a href="/wiki/Jaffna_Lagoon" title="Jaffna Lagoon">Jaffna Lagoon</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_3" title="January 3">January 3</a>
<ul>
<li>In Moscow, Presidents <a href="/wiki/George_H._W._Bush" title="George H. W. Bush">George H. W. Bush</a> (United States) and <a href="/wiki/Boris_Yeltsin" title="Boris Yeltsin">Boris Yeltsin</a> (Russia) sign the <a href="/wiki/START_II" title="START II">second Strategic Arms Reduction Treaty</a>.</li>
<li>The third <i><a href="/wiki/Star_Trek" title="Star Trek">Star Trek</a></i> TV series <i><a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_Deep_Space_Nine" title="Star Trek: Deep Space Nine">Deep Space Nine</a></i> premieres in <a href="/wiki/Broadcast_syndication" title="Broadcast syndication">syndication</a>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_5" title="January 5">January 5</a>
<ul>
<li>The state of <a href="/wiki/Washington_(state)" title="Washington (state)">Washington</a> executes <a href="/wiki/Westley_Allan_Dodd" title="Westley Allan Dodd">Westley Allan Dodd</a> by <a href="/wiki/Hanging" title="Hanging">hanging</a> (the first judicial hanging in America since 1965).</li>
<li>US$7.4 million is stolen from the <a href="/wiki/Brink%27s" title="Brink's">Brink's</a> Armored Car Depot in <a href="/wiki/Rochester,_New_York" title="Rochester, New York">Rochester, New York</a> in the 5th largest robbery in U.S. history. Four men, Samuel Millar, Father Patrick Moloney, former Rochester Police officer Thomas O'Connor, and Charles McCormick, all of whom have ties to the <a href="/wiki/Provisional_Irish_Republican_Army" title="Provisional Irish Republican Army">Provisional Irish Republican Army</a>, are accused.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/MV_Braer" title="MV Braer">MV&#160;<i>Braer</i></a>, a <a href="/wiki/Liberia" title="Liberia">Liberian</a>-registered <a href="/wiki/Oil_tanker" title="Oil tanker">oil tanker</a>, runs aground off the Scottish island of <a href="/wiki/Mainland,_Shetland" title="Mainland, Shetland">Mainland, Shetland</a>, causing a massive oil spill.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_6" title="January 6">January 6</a> – <a href="/wiki/Douglas_Hurd" title="Douglas Hurd">Douglas Hurd</a> is the first high-ranking British official to visit <a href="/wiki/Argentina" title="Argentina">Argentina</a> since the <a href="/wiki/Falklands_War" title="Falklands War">Falklands War</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_6" title="January 6">January 6</a>–<a href="/wiki/January_20" title="January 20">20</a> – The <a href="/wiki/Bombay_Riots" class="mw-redirect" title="Bombay Riots">Bombay Riots</a> take place in <a href="/wiki/Mumbai" title="Mumbai">Mumbai</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_7" title="January 7">January 7</a> – The <a href="/wiki/Fourth_Republic_of_Ghana" class="mw-redirect" title="Fourth Republic of Ghana">Fourth Republic of Ghana</a> is inaugurated, with <a href="/wiki/Jerry_Rawlings" title="Jerry Rawlings">Jerry Rawlings</a> as president.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_8" title="January 8">January 8</a>–<a href="/wiki/January_17" title="January 17">17</a> – The <a href="/wiki/Braer_Storm_of_January_1993" title="Braer Storm of January 1993">Braer Storm of January 1993</a>, the most intense <a href="/wiki/Extratropical_cyclone" title="Extratropical cyclone">extratropical cyclone</a> on record for the northern Atlantic Ocean, occurs.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_11" title="January 11">January 11</a> – <i><a href="/wiki/Monday_Night_Raw" class="mw-redirect" title="Monday Night Raw">Monday Night Raw</a></i>, the longest running weekly episodic show of the World Wrestling Entertainment/Federation (<a href="/wiki/WWE" title="WWE">WWE</a>/F), debuts on television in the United States.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_14" title="January 14">January 14</a> – The Polish ferry <a href="/wiki/MS_Jan_Heweliusz" title="MS Jan Heweliusz">MS&#160;<i>Jan Heweliusz</i></a> sinks off the coast of <a href="/wiki/R%C3%BCgen" title="Rügen">Rügen</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Baltic_Sea" title="Baltic Sea">Baltic Sea</a>, killing 54 people.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_15" title="January 15">January 15</a> – <a href="/wiki/Salvatore_Riina" title="Salvatore Riina">Salvatore Riina</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Sicilian_Mafia" title="Sicilian Mafia">Sicilian Mafia</a> boss known as 'The Beast', is arrested in <a href="/wiki/Palermo" title="Palermo">Palermo</a>, <a href="/wiki/Sicily" title="Sicily">Sicily</a>, after 23 years as a fugitive.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_19" title="January 19">January 19</a>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Chemical_Weapons_Convention" title="Chemical Weapons Convention">Chemical Weapons Convention</a> (CWC) is signed.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/IBM" title="IBM">IBM</a> announces a $4.97 billion loss for 1992, the largest single-year corporate loss in United States history to date.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Iraq_disarmament_crisis" title="Iraq disarmament crisis">Iraq disarmament crisis</a>: <a href="/wiki/Iraq" title="Iraq">Iraq</a> refuses to allow UNSCOM inspectors to use its own aircraft to fly into Iraq, and begins military operations in the demilitarized zone between Iraq and <a href="/wiki/Kuwait" title="Kuwait">Kuwait</a>, and the northern <a href="/wiki/Iraqi_no-fly_zones" title="Iraqi no-fly zones">Iraqi no-fly zones</a>. U.S. forces fire approximately 40 Tomahawk cruise missiles at <a href="/wiki/Baghdad" title="Baghdad">Baghdad</a> factories linked to Iraq's illegal nuclear weapons program. Iraq then informs UNSCOM that it will be able to resume its flights.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_20" title="January 20">January 20</a> – <a href="/wiki/Bill_Clinton" title="Bill Clinton">Bill Clinton</a> is <a href="/wiki/First_inauguration_of_Bill_Clinton" title="First inauguration of Bill Clinton">sworn in</a> as President of the United States.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_24" title="January 24">January 24</a> – In <a href="/wiki/Turkey" title="Turkey">Turkey</a>, thousands protest the murder of journalist <a href="/wiki/U%C4%9Fur_Mumcu" title="Uğur Mumcu">Uğur Mumcu</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_25" title="January 25">January 25</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Mir_Aimal_Kasi" class="mw-redirect" title="Mir Aimal Kasi">Mir Aimal Kasi</a> fires a rifle and kills two employees outside <a href="/wiki/Central_Intelligence_Agency" title="Central Intelligence Agency">Central Intelligence Agency</a> headquarters in <a href="/wiki/Langley,_Virginia" title="Langley, Virginia">Langley, Virginia</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Social_Democrats_(Denmark)" title="Social Democrats (Denmark)">Social Democrat</a> <a href="/wiki/Poul_Nyrup_Rasmussen" title="Poul Nyrup Rasmussen">Poul Nyrup Rasmussen</a> succeeds <a href="/wiki/Conservative_People%27s_Party_(Denmark)" title="Conservative People's Party (Denmark)">Conservative</a> <a href="/wiki/Poul_Schl%C3%BCter" title="Poul Schlüter">Poul Schlüter</a> as <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Denmark" title="Prime Minister of Denmark">Prime Minister of Denmark</a>.</li>
<li>The Russian space station <a href="/wiki/Mir" title="Mir">Mir</a> boasts the first art exhibition in outer space.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-1">[1]</a></sup></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_26" title="January 26">January 26</a> – <a href="/wiki/V%C3%A1clav_Havel" title="Václav Havel">Václav Havel</a> is elected President of the Czech Republic.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="February">February</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1993&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: February">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:152px;"><a href="/wiki/File:WTC_1993_ATF_Commons.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/10/WTC_1993_ATF_Commons.jpg/150px-WTC_1993_ATF_Commons.jpg" width="150" height="101" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/10/WTC_1993_ATF_Commons.jpg/225px-WTC_1993_ATF_Commons.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/10/WTC_1993_ATF_Commons.jpg/300px-WTC_1993_ATF_Commons.jpg 2x" data-file-width="400" data-file-height="268" /></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:WTC_1993_ATF_Commons.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
The aftermath of the <a href="/wiki/World_Trade_Center_bombing" class="mw-redirect" title="World Trade Center bombing">World Trade Center bombing</a>.</div>
</div>
</div>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/February_4" title="February 4">February 4</a> – Members of the right-wing Austrian <a href="/wiki/Freedom_Party_of_Austria" title="Freedom Party of Austria">Freedom Party of Austria</a> split to form the <a href="/wiki/Liberal_Forum" title="Liberal Forum">Liberal Forum</a> in protest against the increasing nationalistic bent of the party.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/February_5" title="February 5">February 5</a> – Belgium becomes a <a href="/wiki/Federal_monarchy" title="Federal monarchy">federal monarchy</a> rather than a <a href="/wiki/Unitary_state" title="Unitary state">unitary</a> <a href="/wiki/Monarchy" title="Monarchy">kingdom</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/February_8" title="February 8">February 8</a> – <a href="/wiki/General_Motors" title="General Motors">General Motors</a> sues <a href="/wiki/NBC" title="NBC">NBC</a>, after <i><a href="/wiki/Dateline_NBC" title="Dateline NBC">Dateline NBC</a></i> allegedly rigged 2 crashes showing that some GM pickups can easily catch fire if hit in certain places. NBC settles the lawsuit the following day.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/February_10" title="February 10">February 10</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Lien_Chan" title="Lien Chan">Lien Chan</a> is named by <a href="/wiki/Lee_Teng-hui" title="Lee Teng-hui">Lee Teng-hui</a> to succeed <a href="/wiki/Hau_Pei-tsun" title="Hau Pei-tsun">Hau Pei-tsun</a> as <a href="/wiki/Premier_of_the_Republic_of_China" title="Premier of the Republic of China">Premier of the Republic of China</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Mani_pulite" title="Mani pulite">Mani pulite</a> scandal: Italian legislator <a href="/wiki/Claudio_Martelli" title="Claudio Martelli">Claudio Martelli</a> resigns, followed by various politicians over the next 2 weeks.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/February_11" title="February 11">February 11</a> – <a href="/wiki/Janet_Reno" title="Janet Reno">Janet Reno</a> is selected by President Clinton as <a href="/wiki/United_States_Attorney_General" title="United States Attorney General">Attorney General of the United States</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/February_12" title="February 12">February 12</a> – Two-year-old <a href="/wiki/Murder_of_James_Bulger" title="Murder of James Bulger">James Bulger</a> is abducted from <a href="/wiki/New_Strand_Shopping_Centre" title="New Strand Shopping Centre">New Strand Shopping Centre</a> by two ten-year-old boys, who later torture and murder him.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/February_14" title="February 14">February 14</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Glafcos_Clerides" title="Glafcos Clerides">Glafcos Clerides</a> defeats incumbent <a href="/wiki/George_Vasiliou" title="George Vasiliou">George Vasiliou</a> in the Cypriot presidential election.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Albert_Zafy" title="Albert Zafy">Albert Zafy</a> defeats <a href="/wiki/Didier_Ratsiraka" title="Didier Ratsiraka">Didier Ratsiraka</a> in the Madagascar presidential election.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/February_17" title="February 17">February 17</a> – A ferry sinks in <a href="/wiki/Haiti" title="Haiti">Haiti</a>, killing approximately 1,215 out of 1,500 passengers.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/February_21" title="February 21">February 21</a> – <a href="/wiki/Star_Fox_(series)" class="mw-redirect" title="Star Fox (series)"><i>Star Fox</i> (series)</a> is released, marking the first 3D Polygonal Star Fox title for the Super Famicom/Super Nintendo Entertainment System smash hit game developed by <a href="/wiki/Nintendo" title="Nintendo">Nintendo</a> with programming assistance by Argonaut Software (currently <a href="/wiki/Argonaut_Games" title="Argonaut Games">Argonaut Games</a>).</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/February_22" title="February 22">February 22</a> – <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_Security_Council_Resolution_808" title="United Nations Security Council Resolution 808">UN Security Council Resolution 808</a> is voted on, deciding that "an international tribunal shall be established" to prosecute violations of international law in <a href="/wiki/Yugoslavia" title="Yugoslavia">Yugoslavia</a>. The tribunal is established on <a href="/wiki/May_25" title="May 25">May 25</a> by <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_Security_Council_Resolution_827" title="United Nations Security Council Resolution 827">Resolution 827</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/February_24" title="February 24">February 24</a> – <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Canada" title="Prime Minister of Canada">Prime Minister of Canada</a> <a href="/wiki/Brian_Mulroney" title="Brian Mulroney">Brian Mulroney</a> resigns amidst political and economic turmoil. <a href="/wiki/Kim_Campbell" title="Kim Campbell">Kim Campbell</a>, his successor, becomes Canada's first female Prime Minister.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/February_26" title="February 26">February 26</a> – <a href="/wiki/World_Trade_Center_bombing" class="mw-redirect" title="World Trade Center bombing">World Trade Center bombing</a>: In New York City, a van bomb parked below the North Tower of the <a href="/wiki/World_Trade_Center_(1973-2001)" class="mw-redirect" title="World Trade Center (1973-2001)">World Trade Center</a> explodes, killing 6 and injuring over 1,000.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/February_28" title="February 28">February 28</a> – <a href="/wiki/Bureau_of_Alcohol,_Tobacco,_Firearms_and_Explosives" title="Bureau of Alcohol, Tobacco, Firearms and Explosives">Bureau of Alcohol, Tobacco, Firearms and Explosives</a> agents raid the <a href="/wiki/Branch_Davidians" title="Branch Davidians">Branch Davidian</a> compound in <a href="/wiki/Waco,_Texas" title="Waco, Texas">Waco, Texas</a>, with a warrant to arrest leader <a href="/wiki/David_Koresh" title="David Koresh">David Koresh</a> on federal firearms violations. Four agents and five Davidians die in the raid and a 51-day standoff begins.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="March">March</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1993&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: March">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_4" title="March 4">March 4</a> – Authorities announce the capture of suspected World Trade Center bombing conspirator <a href="/wiki/Mohammad_Salameh" class="mw-redirect" title="Mohammad Salameh">Mohammad Salameh</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_5" title="March 5">March 5</a> – <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_Macedonia" title="Republic of Macedonia">Macedonian</a> <a href="/wiki/Palair" title="Palair">Palair</a> Flight 305, a <a href="/wiki/Fokker_100" title="Fokker 100">F-100</a> on a flight to <a href="/wiki/Z%C3%BCrich" title="Zürich">Zürich</a>, crashes shortly after take-off from <a href="/wiki/Skopje" title="Skopje">Skopje</a>, killing 83 of the 97 on board.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_8" title="March 8">March 8</a> – The Moon moves into its nearest point to Earth, called perigee, at the same time as its fullest phase of the Lunar Cycle. The Moon appears to be 14% bigger and 30% brighter than the year's other full moons. The next time these two events coincided was in 2008.<sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2">[2]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_11" title="March 11">March 11</a> – <a href="/wiki/Janet_Reno" title="Janet Reno">Janet Reno</a> is confirmed by the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Senate" title="United States Senate">United States Senate</a> and sworn in the next day, becoming the first female Attorney General of the United States.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_12" title="March 12">March 12</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/1993_Bombay_bombings" title="1993 Bombay bombings">1993 Bombay bombings</a>: Several bombs explode in <a href="/wiki/Mumbai" title="Mumbai">Bombay</a>, India, killing 257 and injuring hundreds more.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/North_Korea_nuclear_weapons_program" class="mw-redirect" title="North Korea nuclear weapons program">North Korea nuclear weapons program</a>: <a href="/wiki/North_Korea" title="North Korea">North Korea</a> announces that it plans to withdraw from the <a href="/wiki/Nuclear_Nonproliferation_Treaty" class="mw-redirect" title="Nuclear Nonproliferation Treaty">Nuclear Nonproliferation Treaty</a> and refuses to allow inspectors access to nuclear sites.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_13" title="March 13">March 13</a>–<a href="/wiki/March_15" title="March 15">March 15</a> – The <a href="/wiki/1993_Storm_of_the_Century" title="1993 Storm of the Century">Great Blizzard of 1993</a> strikes the eastern U.S., bringing record snowfall and other severe weather all the way from <a href="/wiki/Cuba" title="Cuba">Cuba</a> to <a href="/wiki/Quebec" title="Quebec">Quebec</a>; it reportedly kills 184.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_13" title="March 13">March 13</a> – <a href="/wiki/Australian_federal_election,_1993" title="Australian federal election, 1993">Australian federal election, 1993</a>: The Australian Labor Party stays in power despite poor economic results.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_17" title="March 17">March 17</a> – The <a href="/wiki/Kurdistan_Workers%27_Party" title="Kurdistan Workers' Party">Kurdistan Workers' Party</a> announces a unilateral <a href="/wiki/Ceasefire" title="Ceasefire">ceasefire</a> in <a href="/wiki/Iraq" title="Iraq">Iraq</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_20" title="March 20">March 20</a> – <a href="/wiki/Warrington_bomb_attacks" title="Warrington bomb attacks">Warrington bomb attacks</a>: A <a href="/wiki/Provisional_Irish_Republican_Army" title="Provisional Irish Republican Army">Provisional Irish Republican Army</a> bomb explodes in <a href="/wiki/Warrington" title="Warrington">Warrington</a> Town Centre and kills 2 children, Jonathan Ball and Tim Parry.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_22" title="March 22">March 22</a> – The <a href="/wiki/Intel" title="Intel">Intel</a> Corporation ships the first <a href="/wiki/P5_(microarchitecture)" title="P5 (microarchitecture)">P5</a> <a href="/wiki/Pentium" title="Pentium">Pentium</a> chips.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_24" title="March 24">March 24</a>
<ul>
<li>The Israeli <a href="/wiki/Knesset" title="Knesset">Knesset</a> elects <a href="/wiki/Ezer_Weizman" title="Ezer Weizman">Ezer Weizman</a> as <a href="/wiki/President_of_Israel" title="President of Israel">President of Israel</a>.</li>
<li>South Africa officially abandons its nuclear weapons programme. President de Klerk announces that the country's 6 warheads had already been dismantled in <a href="/wiki/1989" title="1989">1989</a>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_27" title="March 27">March 27</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jiang_Zemin" title="Jiang Zemin">Jiang Zemin</a> becomes <a href="/wiki/President_of_the_People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="President of the People's Republic of China">President of the People's Republic of China</a>.</li>
<li>Following a rash of <a href="/wiki/Integrism" title="Integrism">integrist</a> murders, <a href="/wiki/Algeria" title="Algeria">Algeria</a> breaks diplomatic relations with <a href="/wiki/Iran" title="Iran">Iran</a>, accusing the country of interfering in its interior affairs.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Mahamane_Ousmane" title="Mahamane Ousmane">Mahamane Ousmane</a> is elected president of <a href="/wiki/Niger" title="Niger">Niger</a>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_28" title="March 28">March 28</a> – <a href="/wiki/French_legislative_election,_1993" title="French legislative election, 1993">French legislative election, 1993</a>: <a href="/wiki/Rally_for_the_Republic" title="Rally for the Republic">Rally for the Republic</a> (Gaullist party) wins a majority and <a href="/wiki/%C3%89douard_Balladur" title="Édouard Balladur">Édouard Balladur</a> becomes <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_France" title="Prime Minister of France">Prime Minister</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_29" title="March 29">March 29</a> – The <a href="/wiki/65th_Academy_Awards" title="65th Academy Awards">65th Academy Awards</a>, hosted by <a href="/wiki/Billy_Crystal" title="Billy Crystal">Billy Crystal</a>, are held at the <a href="/wiki/Dorothy_Chandler_Pavilion" title="Dorothy Chandler Pavilion">Dorothy Chandler Pavilion</a> in <a href="/wiki/Los_Angeles" title="Los Angeles">Los Angeles</a>, with <i><a href="/wiki/Unforgiven" title="Unforgiven">Unforgiven</a></i> winning <a href="/wiki/Academy_Award_for_Best_Picture" title="Academy Award for Best Picture">Best Picture</a>.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="April">April</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1993&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: April">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li>April – The Kuwaiti government claims to uncover an Iraqi assassination plot against former U.S. President <a href="/wiki/George_H._W._Bush" title="George H. W. Bush">George Bush</a> shortly after his visit to Kuwait. Two Iraqi nationals confess to driving a car-bomb into Kuwait on behalf of the <a href="/wiki/Iraqi_Intelligence_Service" title="Iraqi Intelligence Service">Iraqi Intelligence Service</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-3">[3]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/April_1" title="April 1">April 1</a> – The <a href="/wiki/Holy_See" title="Holy See">Vatican</a> orders the moving of the <a href="/wiki/Carmelites" title="Carmelites">Carmelite</a> <a href="/wiki/Convent" title="Convent">convent</a> at <a href="/wiki/Auschwitz_concentration_camp" title="Auschwitz concentration camp">Auschwitz</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/April_6" title="April 6">April 6</a> – A <a href="/wiki/Nuclear_accident" class="mw-redirect" title="Nuclear accident">nuclear accident</a> occurs at <a href="/wiki/Tomsk_7" class="mw-redirect" title="Tomsk 7">Tomsk 7</a> in Russia.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/April_8" title="April 8">April 8</a> – The <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_Macedonia" title="Republic of Macedonia">Republic of Macedonia</a> is admitted to the <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/April_10" title="April 10">April 10</a> – <a href="/wiki/African_National_Congress" title="African National Congress">African National Congress</a> activist <a href="/wiki/Chris_Hani" title="Chris Hani">Chris Hani</a> is assassinated in South Africa.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/April_16" title="April 16">April 16</a> – <a href="/wiki/Bosnian_War" title="Bosnian War">Bosnian War</a>: the enclave of <a href="/wiki/Srebrenica" title="Srebrenica">Srebrenica</a> is declared a UN-protected "safe area".</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/April_19" title="April 19">April 19</a>
<ul>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/Waco_siege" title="Waco siege">51-day stand-off</a> at the Branch Davidian compound near <a href="/wiki/Waco,_Texas" title="Waco, Texas">Waco, Texas</a>, ends with a fire that kills 76 people, including <a href="/wiki/David_Koresh" title="David Koresh">David Koresh</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/South_Dakota" title="South Dakota">South Dakota</a> governor <a href="/wiki/George_S._Mickelson" title="George S. Mickelson">George Mickelson</a> and 7 others are killed when a state-owned aircraft crashes near <a href="/wiki/Dubuque,_Iowa" title="Dubuque, Iowa">Dubuque, Iowa</a>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/April_21" title="April 21">April 21</a> – The Supreme Court in <a href="/wiki/La_Paz" title="La Paz">La Paz</a>, <a href="/wiki/Bolivia" title="Bolivia">Bolivia</a>, sentences former dictator <a href="/wiki/Luis_Garcia_Meza" class="mw-redirect" title="Luis Garcia Meza">Luis Garcia Meza</a> to 30 years in jail without parole for murder, theft, fraud and violating the constitution.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/April_22" title="April 22">April 22</a> – In Washington, D.C., the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Holocaust_Memorial_Museum" title="United States Holocaust Memorial Museum">Holocaust Memorial Museum</a> is dedicated.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/April_23" title="April 23">April 23</a>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/World_Health_Organization" title="World Health Organization">World Health Organization</a> declares <a href="/wiki/Tuberculosis" title="Tuberculosis">tuberculosis</a> a Global Emergency.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Eritrea" title="Eritrea">Eritreans</a> vote overwhelmingly for independence from <a href="/wiki/Ethiopia" title="Ethiopia">Ethiopia</a> in a <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a>-monitored referendum, the <a href="/wiki/Eritrean_independence_referendum,_1993" title="Eritrean independence referendum, 1993">Eritrean independence referendum</a>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/April_24" title="April 24">April 24</a> – A huge <a href="/wiki/Provisional_Irish_Republican_Army" title="Provisional Irish Republican Army">IRA</a> truck bomb explodes at <a href="/wiki/1993_Bishopsgate_bombing" title="1993 Bishopsgate bombing">Bishopsgate</a> in the centre of London's financial district, killing one person and causing extensive damage to the area.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/April_26" title="April 26">April 26</a> – <a href="/wiki/Oscar_Luigi_Scalfaro" title="Oscar Luigi Scalfaro">Oscar Luigi Scalfaro</a> appoints <a href="/wiki/Carlo_Azeglio_Ciampi" title="Carlo Azeglio Ciampi">Carlo Azeglio Ciampi</a> as <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Italy" title="Prime Minister of Italy">Prime Minister of Italy</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/April_27" title="April 27">April 27</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Eritrea" title="Eritrea">Eritrea</a>: Eritrean independence is declared as a result of <a href="/wiki/Eritrean_independence_referendum,_1993" title="Eritrean independence referendum, 1993">a referendum</a> held with <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a> verification.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Yemeni_parliamentary_election,_1993" title="Yemeni parliamentary election, 1993">Yemeni parliamentary election, 1993</a>: The <a href="/wiki/General_People%27s_Congress_(Yemen)" title="General People's Congress (Yemen)">General People's Congress</a> wins a <a href="/wiki/Plurality_(voting)" title="Plurality (voting)">plurality</a> of 121 seats.</li>
<li>All members of the <a href="/wiki/Zambia_national_football_team" title="Zambia national football team">Zambia national football team</a> die in a plane crash off Libreville, Gabon en route to <a href="/wiki/Dakar" title="Dakar">Dakar</a>, <a href="/wiki/Senegal" title="Senegal">Senegal</a>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/April_28" title="April 28">April 28</a> – An executive order requires the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Air_Force" title="United States Air Force">United States Air Force</a> to allow women to fly war planes.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/April_30" title="April 30">April 30</a> – Tennis star <a href="/wiki/Monica_Seles" title="Monica Seles">Monica Seles</a> is stabbed in the back by an obsessed fan of rival <a href="/wiki/Steffi_Graf" title="Steffi Graf">Steffi Graf</a> at a tournament in <a href="/wiki/Hamburg" title="Hamburg">Hamburg</a>, Germany.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="May">May</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1993&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: May">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_1" title="May 1">May 1</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Pierre_B%C3%A9r%C3%A9govoy" title="Pierre Bérégovoy">Pierre Bérégovoy</a>, former <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_France" title="Prime Minister of France">Prime Minister of France</a>, commits suicide.</li>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/Tamil_Tigers" class="mw-redirect" title="Tamil Tigers">Tamil Tigers</a> <a href="/wiki/Suicide_bomber" class="mw-redirect" title="Suicide bomber">suicide bomber</a> assassinates President <a href="/wiki/Ranasinghe_Premadasa" title="Ranasinghe Premadasa">Ranasinghe Premadasa</a> of <a href="/wiki/Sri_Lanka" title="Sri Lanka">Sri Lanka</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Dingiri_Banda_Wijetunga" title="Dingiri Banda Wijetunga">Dingiri Banda Wijetunga</a> became <a href="/wiki/President_of_Sri_Lanka" title="President of Sri Lanka">third executive president</a> of <a href="/wiki/Sri_Lanka" title="Sri Lanka">Sri Lanka</a>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_4" title="May 4">May 4</a> – <a href="/wiki/UNOSOM_II" class="mw-redirect" title="UNOSOM II">UNOSOM II</a> assumes the <a href="/wiki/Somalia" title="Somalia">Somalian</a> duties of the dissolved <a href="/wiki/UNITAF" class="mw-redirect" title="UNITAF">UNITAF</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_9" title="May 9">May 9</a> – <a href="/wiki/Juan_Carlos_Wasmosy" title="Juan Carlos Wasmosy">Juan Carlos Wasmosy</a> becomes the first democratically elected <a href="/wiki/President_of_Paraguay" title="President of Paraguay">President of Paraguay</a> in nearly 40 years.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_15" title="May 15">May 15</a> – <a href="/wiki/Niamh_Kavanagh" title="Niamh Kavanagh">Niamh Kavanagh</a> wins the <a href="/wiki/Eurovision_Song_Contest_1993" title="Eurovision Song Contest 1993">Eurovision Song Contest</a> for Ireland with "<a href="/wiki/In_Your_Eyes_(Niamh_Kavanagh_song)" title="In Your Eyes (Niamh Kavanagh song)">In Your Eyes</a>".</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_16" title="May 16">May 16</a> – The <a href="/wiki/Grand_National_Assembly_of_Turkey" title="Grand National Assembly of Turkey">Grand National Assembly of Turkey</a> elects Prime Minister <a href="/wiki/S%C3%BCleyman_Demirel" title="Süleyman Demirel">Süleyman Demirel</a> as <a href="/wiki/President_of_Turkey" title="President of Turkey">President of Turkey</a>. After Demirel becomes president, the acting <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Turkey" title="Prime Minister of Turkey">Prime Minister of Turkey</a> is <a href="/wiki/Erdal_%C4%B0n%C3%B6n%C3%BC" title="Erdal İnönü">Erdal İnönü</a> of <a href="/wiki/Social_Democratic_Populist_Party_(Turkey)" title="Social Democratic Populist Party (Turkey)">Social Democratic Populist Party</a> for 40 days.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_24" title="May 24">May 24</a> – <a href="/wiki/Eritrea" title="Eritrea">Eritrea</a> gains independence from <a href="/wiki/Ethiopia" title="Ethiopia">Ethiopia</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_25" title="May 25">May 25</a> – The <a href="/wiki/International_Criminal_Tribunal_for_the_former_Yugoslavia" title="International Criminal Tribunal for the former Yugoslavia">International Criminal Tribunal for the former Yugoslavia</a> is created in <a href="/wiki/The_Hague" title="The Hague">The Hague</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_27" title="May 27">May 27</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Massacre_of_Via_dei_Georgofili" class="mw-redirect" title="Massacre of Via dei Georgofili">Massacre of Via dei Georgofili</a>: A car bomb planted outside the <a href="/wiki/Uffizi" title="Uffizi">Uffizi</a> Gallery in <a href="/wiki/Florence" title="Florence">Florence</a> by <a href="/wiki/The_Mafia" class="mw-redirect" title="The Mafia">the Mafia</a> kills 5 and irretrievably destroys 3 paintings.<sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-4">[4]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-5">[5]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Kenneth_Clarke" title="Kenneth Clarke">Kenneth Clarke</a> is appointed Chancellor of the Exchequer in <a href="/wiki/John_Major" title="John Major">John Major</a>'s parliament, after Major sacked <a href="/wiki/Norman_Lamont" title="Norman Lamont">Norman Lamont</a> following <a href="/wiki/Black_Wednesday" title="Black Wednesday">Black Wednesday</a>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_28" title="May 28">May 28</a>
<ul>
<li>Eritrea and <a href="/wiki/Monaco" title="Monaco">Monaco</a> gain entry to the United Nations.</li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Super_Mario_Bros._(film)" title="Super Mario Bros. (film)">Super Mario Bros.</a></i>, the first major American movie based on a video game, is released in theaters.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_29" title="May 29">May 29</a> – The first <a href="/wiki/Life_Ball" title="Life Ball">Life Ball</a> takes place in Vienna, Austria. In 2011, the event is named the largest public charity on HIV and AIDS in Europe.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="June">June</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1993&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: June">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/June_1" title="June 1">June 1</a>
<ul>
<li>Large protests erupt against <a href="/wiki/Slobodan_Milo%C5%A1evi%C4%87" title="Slobodan Milošević">Slobodan Milošević</a>'s regime in <a href="/wiki/Belgrade" title="Belgrade">Belgrade</a>; opposition leader <a href="/wiki/Vuk_Dra%C5%A1kovi%C4%87" title="Vuk Drašković">Vuk Drašković</a> and his wife Danica are arrested.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/President_of_Guatemala" title="President of Guatemala">President of Guatemala</a> <a href="/wiki/Jorge_Serrano_El%C3%ADas" title="Jorge Serrano Elías">Jorge Serrano Elías</a> is forced to flee the country after an attempted <a href="/wiki/Self-coup" title="Self-coup">self-coup</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Burundian_presidential_election,_1993" title="Burundian presidential election, 1993">Burundian presidential election, 1993</a>: The first multiparty elections in Burundi since the country's independence lead to the election of <a href="/wiki/Melchior_Ndadaye" title="Melchior Ndadaye">Melchior Ndadaye</a>, leader of the <a href="/wiki/Front_for_Democracy_in_Burundi" title="Front for Democracy in Burundi">Front for Democracy in Burundi</a>. The next day's <a href="/wiki/Burundian_legislative_election,_1993" title="Burundian legislative election, 1993">legislative election</a> sees his party win with an overwhelming majority.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/June_5" title="June 5">June 5</a>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/National_Assembly_of_Venezuela" class="mw-redirect" title="National Assembly of Venezuela">National Assembly of Venezuela</a> designates <a href="/wiki/Ram%C3%B3n_Jos%C3%A9_Vel%C3%A1squez" title="Ramón José Velásquez">Ramón José Velásquez</a> as successor of suspended <a href="/wiki/President_of_Venezuela" title="President of Venezuela">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Carlos_Andr%C3%A9s_P%C3%A9rez" title="Carlos Andrés Pérez">Carlos Andrés Pérez</a>.</li>
<li>24 <a href="/wiki/Pakistan" title="Pakistan">Pakistani</a> troops in the <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a> forces are killed in <a href="/wiki/Mogadishu" title="Mogadishu">Mogadishu</a>, <a href="/wiki/Somalia" title="Somalia">Somalia</a>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/June_6" title="June 6">June 6</a>
<ul>
<li>Following the <a href="/wiki/Revolutionary_Nationalist_Movement" title="Revolutionary Nationalist Movement">Revolutionary Nationalist Movement</a>'s victory, <a href="/wiki/Gonzalo_S%C3%A1nchez_de_Lozada" title="Gonzalo Sánchez de Lozada">Gonzalo Sánchez de Lozada</a> becomes president of Bolivia.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Mongolia" title="Mongolia">Mongolia</a> holds its first direct presidential elections.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/June_8" title="June 8">June 8</a> – The PKK-declared ceasefire ends in <a href="/wiki/Iraq" title="Iraq">Iraq</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/June_14" title="June 14">June 14</a> – Multipartyists win a referendum on the future of the one-party system in <a href="/wiki/Malawi" title="Malawi">Malawi</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/June_18" title="June 18">June 18</a> – <a href="/wiki/Iraq_disarmament_crisis" title="Iraq disarmament crisis">Iraq disarmament crisis</a>: Iraq refuses to allow UNSCOM weapons inspectors to install remote-controlled monitoring cameras at two missile engine test stands.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/June_20" title="June 20">June 20</a> – <a href="/wiki/John_Paxson" title="John Paxson">John Paxson</a>'s 3-point shot in game six of the NBA Finals helps the <a href="/wiki/Chicago_Bulls" title="Chicago Bulls">Chicago Bulls</a> secure a 99–98 win over the <a href="/wiki/Phoenix_Suns" title="Phoenix Suns">Phoenix Suns</a>, and their third consecutive championship.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/June_22" title="June 22">June 22</a> – Japan's <a href="/wiki/New_Party_Sakigake" title="New Party Sakigake">New Party Sakigake</a> breaks away from the <a href="/wiki/Liberal_Democratic_Party_(Japan)" title="Liberal Democratic Party (Japan)">Liberal Democratic Party</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/June_23" title="June 23">June 23</a> – In <a href="/wiki/Manassas,_Virginia" title="Manassas, Virginia">Manassas, Virginia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Lorena_Bobbitt" class="mw-redirect" title="Lorena Bobbitt">Lorena Bobbitt</a> cuts off the penis of her husband <a href="/wiki/John_Wayne_Bobbitt" class="mw-redirect" title="John Wayne Bobbitt">John Wayne Bobbitt</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/June_24" title="June 24">June 24</a>
<ul>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/Unabomber" class="mw-redirect" title="Unabomber">Unabomber</a> bomb injures computer scientist <a href="/wiki/David_Gelernter" title="David Gelernter">David Gelernter</a> at <a href="/wiki/Yale_University" title="Yale University">Yale University</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Andrew_Wiles" title="Andrew Wiles">Andrew Wiles</a> wins worldwide fame after presenting his proof of <a href="/wiki/Fermat%27s_Last_Theorem" title="Fermat's Last Theorem">Fermat's Last Theorem</a>, a problem that had been unsolved for more than three centuries.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/June_25" title="June 25">June 25</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Kim_Campbell" title="Kim Campbell">Kim Campbell</a> becomes the 19th, and first female, <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Canada" title="Prime Minister of Canada">Prime Minister of Canada</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Tansu_%C3%87iller" title="Tansu Çiller">Tansu Çiller</a> of <a href="/wiki/True_Path_Party_(Turkey)" class="mw-redirect" title="True Path Party (Turkey)">True Path Party</a> forms the new government of <a href="/wiki/Turkey" title="Turkey">Turkey</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Zoran_Lili%C4%87" title="Zoran Lilić">Zoran Lilić</a> succeeds <a href="/wiki/Dobrica_%C4%86osi%C4%87" title="Dobrica Ćosić">Dobrica Ćosić</a> as <a href="/wiki/President_of_Yugoslavia" title="President of Yugoslavia">President of Yugoslavia</a>.</li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Lithuanian_litas" title="Lithuanian litas">litas</a> is introduced in <a href="/wiki/Lithuania" title="Lithuania">Lithuania</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jacques_Attali" title="Jacques Attali">Jacques Attali</a> resigns as President of the <a href="/wiki/European_Bank_for_Reconstruction_and_Development" title="European Bank for Reconstruction and Development">European Bank for Reconstruction and Development</a>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/June_26" title="June 26">June 26</a>–<a href="/wiki/June_28" title="June 28">June 28</a> – <a href="/wiki/Typhoon_Koryn_(1993)" title="Typhoon Koryn (1993)">Typhoon Koryn</a> causes massive damage to the <a href="/wiki/Philippines" title="Philippines">Philippines</a>, China and <a href="/wiki/Macau" title="Macau">Macau</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/June_27" title="June 27">June 27</a>
<ul>
<li>U.S. President <a href="/wiki/Bill_Clinton" title="Bill Clinton">Bill Clinton</a> orders a <a href="/wiki/Cruise_missile_strikes_on_Iraq_(June_1993)" class="mw-redirect" title="Cruise missile strikes on Iraq (June 1993)">cruise missile attack on Iraqi intelligence headquarters</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Al-Mansur" title="Al-Mansur">Al-Mansur</a> District of <a href="/wiki/Baghdad" title="Baghdad">Baghdad</a>, in response to an Iraqi plot to assassinate former U.S. President <a href="/wiki/George_H._W._Bush" title="George H. W. Bush">George H. W. Bush</a> during his visit to Kuwait in mid-April.</li>
<li>In Bad Kleinen, Germany, <a href="/wiki/GSG_9" title="GSG 9">GSG 9</a> troopers arrest <a href="/wiki/Birgit_Hogefeld" title="Birgit Hogefeld">Birgit Hogefeld</a> and kill <a href="/wiki/Wolfgang_Grams" title="Wolfgang Grams">Wolfgang Grams</a>, two <a href="/wiki/Red_Army_Faction" title="Red Army Faction">Red Army Faction</a> terrorists.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="July">July</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1993&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: July">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_2" title="July 2">July 2</a>
<ul>
<li>An integrist mob sets fire to the hotel where <i><a href="/wiki/The_Satanic_Verses" title="The Satanic Verses">The Satanic Verses</a></i> translator <a href="/wiki/Aziz_Nesin" title="Aziz Nesin">Aziz Nesin</a> resides in <a href="/wiki/Sivas" title="Sivas">Sivas</a>, <a href="/wiki/Turkey" title="Turkey">Turkey</a>, killing 37.</li>
<li>266 people died after a floating chapel, sank in <a href="/wiki/Bocaue" class="mw-redirect" title="Bocaue">Bocaue</a>, <a href="/wiki/Bulacan" title="Bulacan">Bulacan</a>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_5" title="July 5">July 5</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Iraq_disarmament_crisis" title="Iraq disarmament crisis">Iraq disarmament crisis</a>: UN inspection teams leave Iraq. Iraq then agrees to <a href="/wiki/UNSCOM" class="mw-redirect" title="UNSCOM">UNSCOM</a> demands and the inspection teams return.</li>
<li>Electrochemist <a href="/wiki/Faiza_Al-Kharafi" title="Faiza Al-Kharafi">Faiza Al-Kharafi</a> is appointed rector (president) of <a href="/wiki/Kuwait_University" title="Kuwait University">Kuwait University</a>, the first woman to head a major university in the Middle East.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_7" title="July 7">July 7</a>–<a href="/wiki/July_9" title="July 9">July 9</a> – The <a href="/wiki/19th_G7_summit" title="19th G7 summit">19th G7 summit</a> is held in Tokyo, Japan.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_7" title="July 7">July 7</a> – <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Calvin_(1993)" title="Hurricane Calvin (1993)">Hurricane Calvin</a> lands in Mexico. It is the second Pacific hurricane on record to land in Mexico in July, and kills 34.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_12" title="July 12">July 12</a> – A <a href="/wiki/Richter_magnitude_scale" title="Richter magnitude scale">magnitude</a> 7.8 <a href="/wiki/1993_Hokkaid%C5%8D_earthquake" title="1993 Hokkaidō earthquake">earthquake off Hokkaidō</a>, Japan launches a devastating <a href="/wiki/Tsunami" title="Tsunami">tsunami</a> that kills 202 on the small island of <a href="/wiki/Okushiri,_Hokkaido" title="Okushiri, Hokkaido">Okushiri, Hokkaido</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_16" title="July 16">July 16</a>–<a href="/wiki/July_17" title="July 17">17</a> – In <a href="/wiki/Estonia" title="Estonia">Estonia</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Russians_in_Estonia" title="Russians in Estonia">majority Russian</a> cities of <a href="/wiki/Narva" title="Narva">Narva</a> and <a href="/wiki/Sillam%C3%A4e" title="Sillamäe">Sillamäe</a> organize referendums on "territorial autonomy" to protest new citizenship laws. The referendums are later declared null and void by the Supreme Court.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_19" title="July 19">July 19</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Japanese_general_election,_1993" title="Japanese general election, 1993">Japanese general election, 1993</a>: The loss of majority of the Liberal Democratic Party results in a coalition taking power.</li>
<li>U.S. President Bill Clinton announces his '<a href="/wiki/Don%27t_ask,_don%27t_tell" title="Don't ask, don't tell">Don't ask, don't tell</a>' policy regarding gays in the American military.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_20" title="July 20">July 20</a> – <a href="/wiki/White_House" title="White House">White House</a> deputy counsel <a href="/wiki/Vince_Foster" title="Vince Foster">Vince Foster</a> commits suicide in Virginia.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_23" title="July 23">July 23</a> – <a href="/wiki/Candel%C3%A1ria_massacre" title="Candelária massacre">Candelária massacre</a>: Brazilian police officers kill eight street kids in <a href="/wiki/Rio_de_Janeiro" title="Rio de Janeiro">Rio de Janeiro</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_26" title="July 26">July 26</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Miguel_Indurain" title="Miguel Indurain">Miguel Indurain</a> wins the <a href="/wiki/1993_Tour_de_France" title="1993 Tour de France">1993 Tour de France</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Asiana_Airlines_Flight_733" title="Asiana Airlines Flight 733">Asiana Airlines Flight 733</a> crashes into Mt. Ungeo in <a href="/wiki/Haenam" class="mw-redirect" title="Haenam">Haenam</a>, South Korea; 68 die.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_27" title="July 27">July 27</a> – <a href="/wiki/Windows_NT_3.1" title="Windows NT 3.1">Windows NT 3.1</a>, the first version of <a href="/wiki/Microsoft" title="Microsoft">Microsoft</a>'s line of <a href="/wiki/Windows_NT" title="Windows NT">Windows NT</a> operating systems, is released to manufacturing.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_29" title="July 29">July 29</a> – The <a href="/wiki/Israeli_Supreme_Court" class="mw-redirect" title="Israeli Supreme Court">Israeli Supreme Court</a> acquits accused <a href="/wiki/Nazi" class="mw-redirect" title="Nazi">Nazi</a> death camp guard <a href="/wiki/John_Demjanjuk" title="John Demjanjuk">John Demjanjuk</a> of all charges and he is set free.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="August">August</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1993&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: August">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_4" title="August 4">August 4</a>
<ul>
<li>A federal judge sentences <a href="/wiki/Los_Angeles_Police_Department" title="Los Angeles Police Department">Los Angeles Police Department</a> officers <a href="/wiki/Stacey_Koon" title="Stacey Koon">Stacey Koon</a> and Laurence Powell to 30 months in prison for violating motorist <a href="/wiki/Rodney_King" title="Rodney King">Rodney King</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Civil_and_political_rights" title="Civil and political rights">civil rights</a>.</li>
<li>The Japanese government issues the Kono Statement, acknowledging the <a href="/wiki/Comfort_women" title="Comfort women">comfort women</a>'s (sex slaves) deportation.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_5" title="August 5">August 5</a>
<ul>
<li>The discovery of the <a href="/wiki/Tel_Dan_Stele" title="Tel Dan Stele">Tel Dan Stele</a>, the first archaeological confirmation of the existence of the <a href="/wiki/Davidic_line" title="Davidic line">Davidic line</a>, is announced.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Magic:_The_Gathering" title="Magic: The Gathering">Magic: The Gathering</a> undergoes its first general release.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_6" title="August 6">August 6</a> – According to <a href="/wiki/Japanese_government" class="mw-redirect" title="Japanese government">Japanese government</a> and <a href="/wiki/Tokyo_Broadcasting_System" title="Tokyo Broadcasting System">TBS</a> networks reports, <a href="/wiki/List_of_natural_disasters_by_death_toll#Storms_.28Non_cyclone.29" title="List of natural disasters by death toll">torrential rain and mudslides</a> kill 72 in <a href="/wiki/Kagoshima" title="Kagoshima">Kagoshima</a>, Japan.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_9" title="August 9">August 9</a> – King <a href="/wiki/Albert_II_of_Belgium" title="Albert II of Belgium">Albert II of Belgium</a> is sworn into office nine days after the death of his brother, King <a href="/wiki/Baudouin_of_Belgium" title="Baudouin of Belgium">Baudouin I</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_13" title="August 13">August 13</a> – Over 130 die in the collapse of Royal Plaza Hotel at <a href="/wiki/Nakhon_Ratchasima" title="Nakhon Ratchasima">Nakhon Ratchasima</a> in <a href="/wiki/Thailand" title="Thailand">Thailand</a>'s worst hotel disaster.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_16" title="August 16">August 16</a> – <a href="/wiki/Debian" title="Debian">Debian</a> announced, initially called "the Debian Linux Release".</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_17" title="August 17">August 17</a> – For the first time, the public is allowed inside <a href="/wiki/Buckingham_Palace" title="Buckingham Palace">Buckingham Palace</a> in London.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_18" title="August 18">August 18</a> – The 14th century <a href="/wiki/Kapellbr%C3%BCcke" title="Kapellbrücke">Kapellbrücke</a> covered wooden <a href="/wiki/Truss_bridge" title="Truss bridge">truss bridge</a> in <a href="/wiki/Lucerne" title="Lucerne">Lucerne</a> (Switzerland) is largely destroyed by fire.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_21" title="August 21">August 21</a> – <a href="/wiki/NASA" title="NASA">NASA</a> loses radio contact with the <a href="/wiki/Mars_Observer" title="Mars Observer">Mars Observer</a> orbiter 3 days before the spacecraft is scheduled to enter orbit around <a href="/wiki/Mars" title="Mars">Mars</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_28" title="August 28">August 28</a> – <a href="/wiki/Ong_Teng_Cheong" title="Ong Teng Cheong">Ong Teng Cheong</a> becomes the first <a href="/wiki/President_of_Singapore" title="President of Singapore">President of Singapore</a> elected by the population.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_28" title="August 28">August 28</a> – <i><a href="/wiki/Mighty_Morphin_Power_Rangers" title="Mighty Morphin Power Rangers">Mighty Morphin Power Rangers</a></i>, one of the longest running and most popular science fiction franchises, debuts on <a href="/wiki/Fox_Kids" title="Fox Kids">Fox Kids</a> with the episode <a href="/wiki/Day_of_the_Dumpster" title="Day of the Dumpster">Day of the Dumpster</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_31" title="August 31">August 31</a> – Russia completes removing its troops from <a href="/wiki/Lithuania" title="Lithuania">Lithuania</a>.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="September">September</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1993&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: September">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:252px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Bill_Clinton,_Yitzhak_Rabin,_Yasser_Arafat_at_the_White_House_1993-09-13.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f2/Bill_Clinton%2C_Yitzhak_Rabin%2C_Yasser_Arafat_at_the_White_House_1993-09-13.jpg/250px-Bill_Clinton%2C_Yitzhak_Rabin%2C_Yasser_Arafat_at_the_White_House_1993-09-13.jpg" width="250" height="171" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f2/Bill_Clinton%2C_Yitzhak_Rabin%2C_Yasser_Arafat_at_the_White_House_1993-09-13.jpg/375px-Bill_Clinton%2C_Yitzhak_Rabin%2C_Yasser_Arafat_at_the_White_House_1993-09-13.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f2/Bill_Clinton%2C_Yitzhak_Rabin%2C_Yasser_Arafat_at_the_White_House_1993-09-13.jpg/500px-Bill_Clinton%2C_Yitzhak_Rabin%2C_Yasser_Arafat_at_the_White_House_1993-09-13.jpg 2x" data-file-width="602" data-file-height="411" /></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
