<a href="/wiki/PLO" class="mw-redirect" title="PLO">PLO</a> leader <a href="/wiki/Yasser_Arafat" title="Yasser Arafat">Yasir Arafat</a> and <a href="/wiki/Israel" title="Israel">Israeli</a> prime minister <a href="/wiki/Yitzhak_Rabin" title="Yitzhak Rabin">Yitzhak Rabin</a>, with US President, <a href="/wiki/Bill_Clinton" title="Bill Clinton">Bill Clinton</a>.</div>
</div>
</div>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/September_13" title="September 13">September 13</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Norwegian_parliamentary_election,_1993" title="Norwegian parliamentary election, 1993">Norwegian parliamentary election, 1993</a>: The Labour Party wins a plurality of the seats, and Prime Minister <a href="/wiki/Gro_Harlem_Brundtland" title="Gro Harlem Brundtland">Gro Harlem Brundtland</a> retains office.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Oslo_I_Accord" title="Oslo I Accord">Oslo I Accord</a>: <a href="/wiki/PLO" class="mw-redirect" title="PLO">PLO</a> leader <a href="/wiki/Yasser_Arafat" title="Yasser Arafat">Yasser Arafat</a> and <a href="/wiki/Israel" title="Israel">Israeli</a> prime minister <a href="/wiki/Yitzhak_Rabin" title="Yitzhak Rabin">Yitzhak Rabin</a> shake hands in Washington, D.C., after signing a peace accord.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/September_15" title="September 15">September 15</a> – <a href="/wiki/Pino_Puglisi" title="Pino Puglisi">Giuseppe 'Pino' Puglisi</a>, an Italian priest in the Palermo neighborhood of Brancaccio, is assassinated in front of his church on his 56th birthday in retaliation for his anti-Mafia activism. One of the hitmen later confessed that Fr. Puglisi's last words as his killers approached were: "I've been expecting you."</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/September_15" title="September 15">September 15</a>–<a href="/wiki/September_21" title="September 21">September 21</a> – <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Gert_(1993)" class="mw-redirect" title="Hurricane Gert (1993)">Hurricane Gert</a> crosses from the Atlantic to the Pacific Ocean through Central America and Mexico.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/September_17" title="September 17">September 17</a> – Russian troops withdraw from Poland.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/September_19" title="September 19">September 19</a> – <a href="/wiki/Polish_parliamentary_election,_1993" title="Polish parliamentary election, 1993">Polish parliamentary election, 1993</a>: A coalition of the <a href="/wiki/Democratic_Left_Alliance" title="Democratic Left Alliance">Democratic Left Alliance</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Polish_People%27s_Party" title="Polish People's Party">Polish People's Party</a> led by <a href="/wiki/Waldemar_Pawlak" title="Waldemar Pawlak">Waldemar Pawlak</a> comes into power.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/September_22" title="September 22">September 22</a> – <a href="/wiki/Big_Bayou_Canot_train_disaster" class="mw-redirect" title="Big Bayou Canot train disaster">Big Bayou Canot train disaster</a>: A bridge collapses as the <i><a href="/wiki/Sunset_Limited" title="Sunset Limited">Sunset Limited</a></i> crosses it, killing 47.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/September_23" title="September 23">September 23</a> – The <a href="/wiki/International_Olympic_Committee" title="International Olympic Committee">International Olympic Committee</a> selects Sydney, Australia to host the <a href="/wiki/2000_Summer_Olympics" title="2000 Summer Olympics">2000 Summer Olympics</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/September_24" title="September 24">September 24</a> – The <a href="/wiki/Cambodia" title="Cambodia">Cambodian</a> monarchy is restored, with <a href="/wiki/Norodom_Sihanouk" title="Norodom Sihanouk">Norodom Sihanouk</a> as king.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/September_26" title="September 26">September 26</a>
<ul>
<li>The first mission in <a href="/wiki/Biosphere_2" title="Biosphere 2">Biosphere 2</a> ends after two years.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/PoSAT-1" title="PoSAT-1">PoSAT-1</a> (the first Portuguese satellite) is launched on board French rocket <a href="/wiki/Ariane_4" title="Ariane 4">Ariane 4</a>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/September_27" title="September 27">September 27</a> – <a href="/wiki/War_in_Abkhazia_(1992%E2%80%9393)" class="mw-redirect" title="War in Abkhazia (1992–93)">War in Abkhazia</a> – <a href="/wiki/Sukhumi_massacre" title="Sukhumi massacre">Fall of Sukhumi</a>: <a href="/wiki/Eduard_Shevardnadze" title="Eduard Shevardnadze">Eduard Shevardnadze</a> accuses Russia of passive complicity.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/September_30" title="September 30">September 30</a> – The 6.2 <a href="/wiki/Moment_magnitude_scale" title="Moment magnitude scale">Mw</a> <a href="/wiki/1993_Latur_earthquake" title="1993 Latur earthquake">Latur earthquake</a> shakes <a href="/wiki/Maharashtra" title="Maharashtra">Maharashtra</a>, India with a maximum <a href="/wiki/Mercalli_intensity_scale" title="Mercalli intensity scale">Mercalli intensity</a> of VIII (<i>Severe</i>) killing 9,748 and injuring 30,000.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="October">October</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1993&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: October">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/October_3" title="October 3">October 3</a> – <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Mogadishu_(1993)" title="Battle of Mogadishu (1993)">Battle of Mogadishu</a>: The U.S. Army conducts <a href="/wiki/Operation_Gothic_Serpent" title="Operation Gothic Serpent">Operation Gothic Serpent</a> in the city of <a href="/wiki/Mogadishu" title="Mogadishu">Mogadishu</a>, Somalia, using <a href="/wiki/Task_Force_Ranger" class="mw-redirect" title="Task Force Ranger">Task Force Ranger</a>. Two U.S. Army <a href="/wiki/UH-60_Blackhawk" class="mw-redirect" title="UH-60 Blackhawk">UH-60 Blackhawks</a> are shot down and the operation leaves over 1,000 Somalians dead and over 73 Americans WIA, 18 KIA, and 1 captured.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/October_4" title="October 4">October 4</a> – The <a href="/wiki/1993_Russian_constitutional_crisis" title="1993 Russian constitutional crisis">Russian constitutional crisis</a> culminates with Russian military and security forces clearing the <a href="/wiki/White_House_of_Russia" class="mw-redirect" title="White House of Russia">White House of Russia</a> Parliament building by force, quashing a mass uprising against President <a href="/wiki/Boris_Yeltsin" title="Boris Yeltsin">Boris Yeltsin</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/October_5" title="October 5">October 5</a>
<ul>
<li>China performs a <a href="/wiki/Nuclear_test" class="mw-redirect" title="Nuclear test">nuclear test</a>, ending a worldwide <i>de facto</i> <a href="/wiki/Moratorium_(law)" title="Moratorium (law)">moratorium</a>.</li>
<li>The papal <a href="/wiki/Encyclical" title="Encyclical">encyclical</a> <i><a href="/wiki/Veritatis_Splendor" class="mw-redirect" title="Veritatis Splendor">Veritatis Splendor</a></i> is promulgated.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/October_10" title="October 10">October 10</a> – The South Korean ferry <i>Seohae</i> capsizes off <a href="/wiki/Pusan" class="mw-redirect" title="Pusan">Pusan</a>, South Korea; 292 are killed.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/October_11" title="October 11">October 11</a>–<a href="/wiki/October_28" title="October 28">October 28</a> – The <a href="/wiki/UNMIH" class="mw-redirect" title="UNMIH">UNMIH</a> is prevented from entering <a href="/wiki/Haiti" title="Haiti">Haiti</a>. On <a href="/wiki/October_18" title="October 18">October 18</a>, economic sanctions (abolished in August) are reinstated.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/October_13" title="October 13">October 13</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Greek_legislative_election,_1993" title="Greek legislative election, 1993">Greek legislative election, 1993</a>: <a href="/wiki/Andreas_Papandreou" title="Andreas Papandreou">Andreas Papandreou</a> begins his second term as <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Greece" title="Prime Minister of Greece">Prime Minister of Greece</a>.</li>
<li>The fifth summit of the <a href="/wiki/Organisation_internationale_de_la_Francophonie" title="Organisation internationale de la Francophonie">Francophonie</a> opens in <a href="/wiki/Mauritius" title="Mauritius">Mauritius</a>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/October_19" title="October 19">October 19</a> – <a href="/wiki/Benazir_Bhutto" title="Benazir Bhutto">Benazir Bhutto</a> becomes the Prime Minister of Pakistan for the second time.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/October_21" title="October 21">October 21</a> – A coup in <a href="/wiki/Burundi" title="Burundi">Burundi</a> results in the death of president <a href="/wiki/Melchior_Ndadaye" title="Melchior Ndadaye">Melchior Ndadaye</a> and sparks the <a href="/wiki/Burundi_Civil_War" class="mw-redirect" title="Burundi Civil War">Burundi Civil War</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/October_25" title="October 25">October 25</a> – <a href="/wiki/Canadian_federal_election,_1993" title="Canadian federal election, 1993">Canadian federal election, 1993</a>: <a href="/wiki/Jean_Chr%C3%A9tien" title="Jean Chrétien">Jean Chrétien</a> and his <a href="/wiki/Liberal_Party_of_Canada" title="Liberal Party of Canada">Liberal Party</a> defeat the governing <a href="/wiki/Progressive_Conservative_Party_of_Canada" title="Progressive Conservative Party of Canada">Progressive Conservative Party</a>, which falls to a historic low of 2 seats.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/October_30" title="October 30">October 30</a> – <a href="/wiki/Greysteel_massacre" title="Greysteel massacre">Greysteel massacre</a>: Three members of the <a href="/wiki/Ulster_Defence_Association" title="Ulster Defence Association">Ulster Defence Association</a>, a loyalist paramilitary group, attack a crowded bar in <a href="/wiki/Greysteel" title="Greysteel">Greysteel</a>, <a href="/wiki/Northern_Ireland" title="Northern Ireland">Northern Ireland</a>, with firearms, killing 8 civilians and wounding 13. The bar was targeted because it is in an Irish nationalist and Catholic area.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="November">November</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1993&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: November">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_1" title="November 1">November 1</a> – The <a href="/wiki/Maastricht_Treaty" title="Maastricht Treaty">Maastricht Treaty</a> takes effect, formally establishing the <a href="/wiki/European_Union" title="European Union">European Union</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_5" title="November 5">November 5</a> – The <a href="/wiki/Parliament_of_the_United_Kingdom" title="Parliament of the United Kingdom">Parliament of the United Kingdom</a> passes the <a href="/wiki/Railways_Act_1993" title="Railways Act 1993">Railways Act 1993</a>, setting out the procedures for <a href="/wiki/Privatisation_of_British_Rail" title="Privatisation of British Rail">privatisation of British Rail</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_9" title="November 9">November 9</a> – <a href="/wiki/Croats_of_Bosnia_and_Herzegovina" title="Croats of Bosnia and Herzegovina">Bosnian Croat</a> forces destroy the <i><a href="/wiki/Stari_Most" title="Stari Most">Stari Most</a></i>, or Old Bridge of <a href="/wiki/Mostar" title="Mostar">Mostar</a>, <a href="/wiki/Bosnia_and_Herzegovina" title="Bosnia and Herzegovina">Bosnia and Herzegovina</a>, by tank fire.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_11" title="November 11">November 11</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Microsoft" title="Microsoft">Microsoft</a> releases <a href="/wiki/Windows_for_Workgroups_3.11" class="mw-redirect" title="Windows for Workgroups 3.11">Windows for Workgroups 3.11</a> to manufacturing.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Sri_Lankan_Civil_War" title="Sri Lankan Civil War">Sri Lankan Civil War</a> – <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Pooneryn" title="Battle of Pooneryn">Battle of Pooneryn</a>: Over 400 Sri Lankan military are killed.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_12" title="November 12">November 12</a> – <a href="/wiki/London_Convention_on_the_Prevention_of_Marine_Pollution_by_Dumping_of_Wastes_and_Other_Matter" title="London Convention on the Prevention of Marine Pollution by Dumping of Wastes and Other Matter">London Convention</a>: Marine dumping of <a href="/wiki/Radioactive_waste" title="Radioactive waste">radioactive waste</a> is outlawed.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_17" title="November 17">November 17</a>–<a href="/wiki/November_22" title="November 22">November 22</a> – The <a href="/wiki/North_American_Free_Trade_Agreement" title="North American Free Trade Agreement">North American Free Trade Agreement</a> (NAFTA) passes the legislative houses in the United States, Canada and Mexico.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_18" title="November 18">November 18</a>
<ul>
<li>In a <a href="/wiki/Puerto_Rican_status_referendums" class="mw-redirect" title="Puerto Rican status referendums">status referendum</a>, <a href="/wiki/Puerto_Rico" title="Puerto Rico">Puerto Rico</a> residents vote with a slim margin to maintain <a href="/wiki/Commonwealth_(U.S._insular_area)" title="Commonwealth (U.S. insular area)">Commonwealth</a> status.</li>
<li>In South Africa, 21 political parties approve a new constitution.</li>
<li>The first meeting of the <a href="/wiki/Asia-Pacific_Economic_Cooperation" title="Asia-Pacific Economic Cooperation">Asia-Pacific Economic Cooperation</a> summit opens in <a href="/wiki/Seattle" title="Seattle">Seattle</a>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_20" title="November 20">November 20</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Savings_and_loan_crisis" title="Savings and loan crisis">Savings and loan crisis</a>: The <a href="/wiki/United_States_Senate_Ethics_Committee" class="mw-redirect" title="United States Senate Ethics Committee">United States Senate Ethics Committee</a> issues a stern censure of <a href="/wiki/California" title="California">California</a> senator <a href="/wiki/Alan_Cranston" title="Alan Cranston">Alan Cranston</a> for his dealings with savings-and-loan executive <a href="/wiki/Charles_Keating" title="Charles Keating">Charles Keating</a>.</li>
<li>An Avioimpex <a href="/wiki/Yakovlev_Yak-42D" class="mw-redirect" title="Yakovlev Yak-42D">Yakovlev Yak-42D</a> crashes into Mount Trojani near <a href="/wiki/Ohrid" title="Ohrid">Ohrid</a>, <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_Macedonia" title="Republic of Macedonia">Macedonia</a>. The aircraft was on a flight from <a href="/wiki/Geneva" title="Geneva">Geneva</a>, Switzerland to Skopje, but had been diverted to Ohrid due to poor weather conditions at the Skopje airport. All 8 crew members and 115 of the 116 passengers are killed.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_28" title="November 28">November 28</a> – <i><a href="/wiki/The_Observer" title="The Observer">The Observer</a></i> reveals that a channel of communications has existed between the <a href="/wiki/Provisional_Irish_Republican_Army" title="Provisional Irish Republican Army">Provisional Irish Republican Army</a> and the British government, despite the government's persistent denials.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_30" title="November 30">November 30</a> – An agreement establishing the Permanent Commission for East African Co-operation is signed. U.S. President <a href="/wiki/Bill_Clinton" title="Bill Clinton">Bill Clinton</a> signs the <a href="/wiki/Brady_Handgun_Violence_Prevention_Act" title="Brady Handgun Violence Prevention Act">Brady Handgun Violence Prevention Act</a>.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="December">December</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1993&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: December">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_1" title="December 1">December 1</a> – A train crash at <a href="/wiki/Tattenham_Corner_railway_station" title="Tattenham Corner railway station">Tattenham Corner railway station</a> leads to the introduction of the current drugs and alcohol policy for railways in the UK.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_2" title="December 2">December 2</a>
<ul>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/STS-61" title="STS-61">STS-61</a></i>: <a href="/wiki/NASA" title="NASA">NASA</a> launches the Space Shuttle <i><a href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle_Endeavour" title="Space Shuttle Endeavour">Endeavour</a></i> on a mission to repair an optical flaw in the <a href="/wiki/Hubble_Space_Telescope" title="Hubble Space Telescope">Hubble Space Telescope</a>.</li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/September_6" title="September 6">September 6</a> merger between <a href="/wiki/Renault" title="Renault">Renault</a> and <a href="/wiki/Volvo" title="Volvo">Volvo</a> fails; Volvo CEO <a href="/wiki/Pehr_G._Gyllenhammar" title="Pehr G. Gyllenhammar">Pehr G. Gyllenhammar</a> resigns.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_5" title="December 5">December 5</a> – <a href="/wiki/Rafael_Caldera_Rodr%C3%ADguez" class="mw-redirect" title="Rafael Caldera Rodríguez">Rafael Caldera Rodríguez</a> is elected President of Venezuela for the second time, succeeding interim president <a href="/wiki/Ram%C3%B3n_Jos%C3%A9_Vel%C3%A1squez" title="Ramón José Velásquez">Ramón José Velásquez</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_7" title="December 7">December 7</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/1993_Long_Island_Rail_Road_shooting" title="1993 Long Island Rail Road shooting">Colin Ferguson opens fire</a> with his Ruger 9&#160;mm pistol on a <a href="/wiki/Long_Island_Rail_Road" title="Long Island Rail Road">Long Island Rail Road</a> train, killing six and injuring 19.</li>
<li>The 32-member Transitional Executive Committee holds its first meeting in <a href="/wiki/Cape_Town" title="Cape Town">Cape Town</a>, marking the first meeting of an official government body in South Africa with Black members.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/List_of_heads_of_state_of_Ivory_Coast" title="List of heads of state of Ivory Coast">President of Ivory Coast</a> <a href="/wiki/F%C3%A9lix_Houphou%C3%ABt-Boigny" title="Félix Houphouët-Boigny">Félix Houphouët-Boigny</a> dies at 88, the oldest African head of state. He is succeeded three days later by <a href="/wiki/Henri_Konan_B%C3%A9di%C3%A9" title="Henri Konan Bédié">Henri Konan Bédié</a>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_8" title="December 8">December 8</a> – U.S. President <a href="/wiki/Bill_Clinton" title="Bill Clinton">Bill Clinton</a> signs into law the <a href="/wiki/North_American_Free_Trade_Agreement" title="North American Free Trade Agreement">North American Free Trade Agreement</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_10" title="December 10">December 10</a> – <a href="/wiki/Id_Software" title="Id Software">id Software</a> releases <i><a href="/wiki/Doom_(1993_video_game)" title="Doom (1993 video game)">Doom</a></i>, a seminal <a href="/wiki/First-person_shooter" title="First-person shooter">first-person shooter</a> that uses advanced <a href="/wiki/3D_computer_graphics" title="3D computer graphics">3D graphics</a> for computer games.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_11" title="December 11">December 11</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Chilean_presidential_election,_1993" class="mw-redirect" title="Chilean presidential election, 1993">Chilean presidential election, 1993</a>: <a href="/wiki/Eduardo_Frei_Ruiz-Tagle" title="Eduardo Frei Ruiz-Tagle">Eduardo Frei Ruiz-Tagle</a> is elected with 58% of the vote.</li>
<li>A variety of <a href="/wiki/Soviet_space_program" title="Soviet space program">Soviet space program</a> paraphernalia are put to auction in <a href="/wiki/Sotheby%27s" title="Sotheby's">Sotheby's</a> New York, and sell for a total of US$6.8M. One of the items is <a href="/wiki/Lunokhod_1" title="Lunokhod 1">Lunokhod 1</a> and its spacecraft <a href="/wiki/Luna_17" title="Luna 17">Luna 17</a>; they sell for $68,500.</li>
<li>One of the three blocks of the Highland Towers near <a href="/wiki/Kuala_Lumpur" title="Kuala Lumpur">Kuala Lumpur</a>, <a href="/wiki/Malaysia" title="Malaysia">Malaysia</a> <a href="/wiki/Highland_Towers_collapse" title="Highland Towers collapse">comes down</a>, killing 48.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_12" title="December 12">December 12</a> – <a href="/wiki/P%C3%A9ter_Boross" title="Péter Boross">Péter Boross</a> becomes <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Hungary" title="Prime Minister of Hungary">Prime Minister of Hungary</a> following the death of <a href="/wiki/J%C3%B3zsef_Antall" title="József Antall">József Antall</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_13" title="December 13">December 13</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Canada" title="Prime Minister of Canada">Prime Minister of Canada</a> <a href="/wiki/Kim_Campbell" title="Kim Campbell">Kim Campbell</a> resigns as leader of the <a href="/wiki/Progressive_Conservative_Party_of_Canada" title="Progressive Conservative Party of Canada">Progressive Conservative Party</a>, and is succeeded as leader by <a href="/wiki/Jean_Charest" title="Jean Charest">Jean Charest</a>.</li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Majilis" class="mw-redirect" title="Majilis">Majilis</a> of <a href="/wiki/Kazakhstan" title="Kazakhstan">Kazakhstan</a> approves the nuclear <a href="/wiki/Non-Proliferation_Treaty" class="mw-redirect" title="Non-Proliferation Treaty">Non-Proliferation Treaty</a>, and agrees to dismantle the more than 100 missiles left on its territory by the fall of the USSR.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_15" title="December 15">December 15</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Downing_Street_Declaration" title="Downing Street Declaration">Downing Street Declaration</a>: The United Kingdom commits itself to the search for an answer to the problems of <a href="/wiki/Northern_Ireland" title="Northern Ireland">Northern Ireland</a>.</li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Uruguay_Round" title="Uruguay Round">Uruguay Round</a> of <a href="/wiki/General_Agreement_on_Tariffs_and_Trade" title="General Agreement on Tariffs and Trade">General Agreement on Tariffs and Trade</a> (GATT) talks reach a successful conclusion after seven years.</li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Schindler%27s_List" title="Schindler's List">Schindler's List</a></i>, directed by <a href="/wiki/Steven_Spielberg" title="Steven Spielberg">Steven Spielberg</a> is released in theatres.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_16" title="December 16">December 16</a> – <a href="/wiki/Brazil" title="Brazil">Brazil</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Supreme_Federal_Court" title="Supreme Federal Court">Supreme Court</a> rules that former President <a href="/wiki/Fernando_Collor_de_Mello" title="Fernando Collor de Mello">Fernando Collor de Mello</a> may not hold elected office again until 2000 due to <a href="/wiki/Political_corruption" title="Political corruption">political corruption</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_18" title="December 18">December 18</a> – <a href="/wiki/Omar_Bongo" title="Omar Bongo">Omar Bongo</a> is re-elected as <a href="/wiki/President_of_Gabon" class="mw-redirect" title="President of Gabon">President of Gabon</a> in the country's first multiparty elections.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_20" title="December 20">December 20</a>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_General_Assembly" title="United Nations General Assembly">United Nations General Assembly</a> votes unanimously to appoint a <a href="/wiki/U.N._High_Commissioner_for_Human_Rights" class="mw-redirect" title="U.N. High Commissioner for Human Rights">U.N. High Commissioner for Human Rights</a>.</li>
<li>The first corrected images from the <a href="/wiki/Hubble_Telescope" class="mw-redirect" title="Hubble Telescope">Hubble Telescope</a> are taken.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_22" title="December 22">December 22</a> – The interim <a href="/wiki/Constitution_of_South_Africa" title="Constitution of South Africa">South African constitution</a> is approved by <a href="/wiki/Parliament_of_South_Africa" title="Parliament of South Africa">Parliament</a> 237–45.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_29" title="December 29">December 29</a> – <a href="/wiki/Argentina" title="Argentina">Argentina</a> passes a measure allowing President <a href="/wiki/Carlos_Menem" title="Carlos Menem">Carlos Menem</a> and all future presidents to run for a second term. It also shortens presidential terms to 4 years and removes the requirement for the president to be <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic" class="mw-redirect" title="Roman Catholic">Roman Catholic</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_30" title="December 30">December 30</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Israel" title="Israel">Israel</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Holy_See" title="Holy See">Vatican</a> establish diplomatic relations.</li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Indian_National_Congress" title="Indian National Congress">Congress Party</a> gains a parliamentary majority in India after the defection of 10 <a href="/wiki/Janata_Dal" title="Janata Dal">Janata Dal</a> party lawmakers.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Date_unknown">Date unknown</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1993&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Date unknown">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li>The second <a href="/wiki/World_Parliament_of_Religions" class="mw-redirect" title="World Parliament of Religions">World Parliament of Religions</a> is held in Chicago.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Michael_Jackson" title="Michael Jackson">Michael Jackson</a> is accused by <a href="/wiki/Evan_Chandler" title="Evan Chandler">Evan Chandler</a> of <a href="/wiki/1993_child_sexual_abuse_accusations_against_Michael_Jackson" title="1993 child sexual abuse accusations against Michael Jackson">sexually molesting</a> Jordan Chandler, Evan's 13-year-old son.</li>
<li>U.S. President Bill Clinton sends 6 American warships to <a href="/wiki/Haiti" title="Haiti">Haiti</a>, to enforce <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a> trade sanctions against the military-led regime in that country.</li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Mississippi_River" title="Mississippi River">Mississippi</a> and <a href="/wiki/Missouri_River" title="Missouri River">Missouri Rivers</a> flood large portions of the <a href="/wiki/Great_Flood_of_1993" title="Great Flood of 1993">American Midwest</a>.</li>
<li>Severe floods hit South Asia, killing over 4,000 people in <a href="/wiki/Bangladesh" title="Bangladesh">Bangladesh</a>, India and <a href="/wiki/Nepal" title="Nepal">Nepal</a>.</li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/European_Exchange_Rate_Mechanism" title="European Exchange Rate Mechanism">European Exchange Rate Mechanism</a> is put in crisis, mainly from <a href="/wiki/Speculation" title="Speculation">speculation</a> against the <a href="/wiki/French_franc" title="French franc">French franc</a>.</li>
<li>Over a dozen people are killed by the new <a href="/wiki/Hantavirus#Hantavirus_.28cardio-.29pulmonary_syndrome" title="Hantavirus">Hantavirus cardiopulmonary syndrome</a>, mainly in the <a href="/wiki/Southwestern_United_States" title="Southwestern United States">Southwestern United States</a>.</li>
<li>Wildfires in <a href="/wiki/California" title="California">California</a> destroy over 16,000 acres (65&#160;km<sup>2</sup>) and 700 homes.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Stephen_Hawking" title="Stephen Hawking">Stephen Hawking</a>'s <i><a href="/wiki/A_Brief_History_of_Time" title="A Brief History of Time">A Brief History of Time</a></i> becomes the longest-running book on the bestseller list of <i><a href="/wiki/The_Sunday_Times" title="The Sunday Times">The Sunday Times</a></i> ever.</li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Oslo_Accords" title="Oslo Accords">Oslo Accords</a> negotiations begin.</li>
<li>Many foreigners are murdered by rebel groups in <a href="/wiki/Algeria" title="Algeria">Algeria</a>.</li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Campaign_for_Homosexual_Law_Reform" title="Campaign for Homosexual Law Reform">Campaign for Homosexual Law Reform</a> succeeds in having the Irish <a href="/wiki/Sodomy_law" title="Sodomy law">sodomy law</a> reformed.</li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/1993_Jack_in_the_Box_E._coli_outbreak" title="1993 Jack in the Box E. coli outbreak">Jack in the Box E.coli</a> Incident occurred in 1993 when 732 people were infected with the Escherichia coli O157:H7 bacterium originating from undercooked beef patties in hamburgers.</li>
<li>The genus <a href="/wiki/Prosansanosmilus" title="Prosansanosmilus">Prosansanosmilus</a> was discovered and classified with its type species, <a href="/wiki/Prosansanosmilus_peregrinus" title="Prosansanosmilus peregrinus">Prosansanosmilus peregrinus</a>.</li>
<li>The DFA-2 gene was discovered.</li>
</ul>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Nobel_Prizes">Nobel Prizes</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1993&amp;action=edit&amp;section=41" title="Edit section: Nobel Prizes">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="floatright"><a href="/wiki/File:Nobel_medal.png" class="image"><img alt="Nobel medal.png" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/6/6a/Nobel_medal.png/100px-Nobel_medal.png" width="100" height="100" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/6/6a/Nobel_medal.png/150px-Nobel_medal.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/6/6a/Nobel_medal.png/200px-Nobel_medal.png 2x" data-file-width="1013" data-file-height="1013" /></a></div>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Nobel_Prize_in_Chemistry" title="Nobel Prize in Chemistry">Chemistry</a> – <a href="/wiki/Kary_Mullis" title="Kary Mullis">Kary Mullis</a>, <a href="/wiki/Michael_Smith_(chemist)" title="Michael Smith (chemist)">Michael Smith</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Nobel_Memorial_Prize_in_Economic_Sciences" title="Nobel Memorial Prize in Economic Sciences">Economics</a> – <a href="/wiki/Robert_W._Fogel" class="mw-redirect" title="Robert W. Fogel">Robert W. Fogel</a>, <a href="/wiki/Douglass_North" title="Douglass North">Douglass North</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Nobel_Prize_in_Literature" title="Nobel Prize in Literature">Literature</a> – <a href="/wiki/Toni_Morrison" title="Toni Morrison">Toni Morrison</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Nobel_Peace_Prize" title="Nobel Peace Prize">Peace</a> – <a href="/wiki/Nelson_Mandela" title="Nelson Mandela">Nelson Mandela</a> and <a href="/wiki/F._W._de_Klerk" title="F. W. de Klerk">Frederik Willem de Klerk</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Nobel_Prize_in_Physics" title="Nobel Prize in Physics">Physics</a> – <a href="/wiki/Russell_Alan_Hulse" title="Russell Alan Hulse">Russell Alan Hulse</a>, <a href="/wiki/Joseph_Hooton_Taylor,_Jr." class="mw-redirect" title="Joseph Hooton Taylor, Jr.">Joseph Hooton Taylor, Jr.</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Nobel_Prize_in_Physiology_or_Medicine" title="Nobel Prize in Physiology or Medicine">Physiology or Medicine</a> – <a href="/wiki/Richard_J._Roberts" title="Richard J. Roberts">Richard J. Roberts</a>, <a href="/wiki/Phillip_Allen_Sharp" title="Phillip Allen Sharp">Phillip Allen Sharp</a></li>
</ul>
